   < 4250c32, Brian Peters, 2022-12-13 14:03:35 -0500 >
   - PWEB-2710: add support for outbound SIP uri dialing in WebLine.makeCall() 
   - in WebLine.makeCall(), detect when dial address is a SIP uri, and avoid test for "Hookflash"
- in WebCall.processAddress(), detect when dial address is a SIP uri, and skip tokenizing address. Instead, use the SIP uri as the token to dial and mark the processed address as a sipUri in the returned data
- in WebCall.dialOnCall(), when processed address is a sip uri, dial to the new 'linepool' destination, and add the new "Linepool:" sip header to the extraHeaders sent to the WebPhone to include in the SIP INVITE request.
- Update WebTeletest to detect the SIP uri dial case and make sure the "dialingPrefix" includes the linepool access code provided by the GUI in the "localPrefix" parameter.

   < 5fa536e, Stephane Legris, 2022-06-03 09:43:08 -0400 >
   - PWEB-2391/PWEB-2401: Add new SIP Register and, an outgoing SIP BYE header. 
   PWEB-2391: The new SIP REGISTER header called "x-CallReofferRequired" will be process by the node to REOFFER all calls related to that position after a WebRTCGw switch over connection.

PWEB-2401: Add a new SIP header called "x-IgnoreBye" when terminating the session.  This new header will be processed by "sip.js" when terminating sessions of the failed WebRTCGw client in order to terminate cleanly all the sessions without sending the SIP BYE.
Please note the SIP BYE, if reaching the node, will terminate the 911 call which we want to keep alive.  This situation may occurs if the WebRTCGw network connection is CUT for a short period of time..

   < d3895d6, etran, 2022-03-23 15:33:23 -0400 >
   - Automatic build TelephonySaaS 1.5.0.6 
   
   < 4e38119, Brian Peters, 2022-03-23 14:20:04 -0400 >
   - PWEB-2085: remove state transition to IHold when connecting consultation call to held conference 
   - when connecting a consultation call from a Normal (sameline) conference, the order of operations is for the consultation call to join the conference, and to UnHold the conference.
- This means the consultation call was going from Connected state in the private consultation conference, to IHold when joining the main conference, to Connected again once the main conference is re-connected (unhold).
- The additional temporary state transition to IHold was causing issued at the P911 GUI level, because no call in the conference was considered "Connected" for a brief moment, and triggered a cleanup of state.
- To avoid this, the consulation call will remain in the Connected state in the on-hold conference, even if this is internally inconsistent, since we know it will become consistent again once all the other calls are Connected by the confernence UnHold at the end of the conference Connect() operation

   < 615c450, Brian Peters, 2022-02-23 08:28:52 -0500 >
   - PWEB-1844: improve LineLock race condition handling in WebCall.answer() 
   - add 500ms delay to callTerminated() promise handling in WebCall.answer() to allow for CallLink event to arrive, which will tell us if LineLock happened
- re-validate the call state after the async operation to hold current connected calls, and Listen & Join cancel, since the state may have changed
- add another level of try/catch for better cleanup of ForceConnectSync
- while testing, we noticed that the SIP.js library didn't always properly handle the race condition of sending the 200 OK from accept() while being Cancelled from the server. In some cases, the call to invitation.accept() promise *never resolves*, which caused our WebPhone.answer() wrapper to also never resolve and leave the app in a state where it could no longer accept calls. A timeout for the WebPhone.answer() was added in WebCall.answer() so the operation always resolves and proper cleanup is done
- in WebLineDev.processCallIncoming(), which is not async, catch the exceptions from the async calls to webCall.reject() and WebCall.answer() and log them

   - Automatic build TelephonySaaS 1.2.0.25 
   
   < 7117d37, Michael Ma, 2021-08-04 14:24:50 -0400 >
   - PWEB-1643, this commit is to avoid throwing exception "NotExist" on AcdLogOff 
   	- A rare and unusual situaion is seen in single node that Voip
	  probably cleaned up its ACD database prior to acdLogout
	  request. This might be because the webClient is pausing and
	  blocking Sip options to send so that Asterisk thinks it's not
	  reachable then cleaned-up database instead. If the web client
	  operates ACD logOff, the Vcc response 'NotExist' will be
	  received and it triggers an exception. This result could
	  potentially prevent PWEB GUI from exit on clicking shutdown
	  button. Response 'NotExist' can be considered as a success of ACD
	  logoff. Since Asterisk does have a seperate way to clean-up
	  its database, we need to take this unusual case as a possibility
	  to cover, which do not throw exception when it's resulted by
	  logout operation
	- Same logic applied to rgLougout in telephony code
	- Also add 'Unknown' ACD and RG opStatus to replace the case of
	  throwing exception if none of pre-defined status in
	  telephony matches what is recieved in the response of ACD or
	  RG OP

   < 7a5eb18, Stephane Legris, 2021-07-29 15:44:57 -0400 >
   - [L&J] PWEB-1579 Resubscribe expires is now 1h 
   
   < b818c4b, Stephane Legris, 2021-07-29 15:17:13 -0400 >
   - [L&J] PWEB-1579: Resubscribe alternative solution 
   - The NTimer or expires is now set to 1h..  Therefore, the L&J will last 1h+ before terminating
- When subscribe unexpected terminated state is received, we terminate the current call if applicable, unsubscribe all nodes BUT, we DO NOT reset current L&J and, DO NOT report event status to the GUI
- Then, we silently start a new monitoring with the same L&J settings.  If a L&J monitoring call was active, the node will then send another NOTIFY to re-establish the call to listen or join the position or AgentID to monitor.
- The whole recovery cycle transition takes about 4-5 seconds.  So, the supervisor will stop earring the position or AgentID for that duration.
- When that L&J re-cycle occurs. The following ERROR message is displayed on the console:  "subscribe <index> UNEXPECTEDLY terminated.  Restart it silently !
- Also, if by any chance, a L&J subscribe is kept alive within a Node, the next subscribe will destroy it.  Furthermore, if a notify is sent by this node, PWEB returns a “481 dialog does not exist”.

   < c8af719, Michael Ma, 2021-03-05 15:49:23 -0500 >
   - PWEB-1196 This commit adds support for multiple VCC GW 
   	- Add VccConnectionHandler to Telephony
	- VccConnectionHandler initally establishes a handles list. Each
	  handle represents the connection and vccClient to a VccGW
	  respectively. It connects/re-connects and creates vccClient and
	  update to lineDev to be effective immediately once it's chosen
	- When a connection close discovered, try with the rest handles in
	  the list at the order of what is configured. The handle to the
	  conection that was just closed is excluded from rest handles list
	  unless it's the only one configured in the system
	- All failure will rerult in a retry over the handles list every
	  10 seconds until one got connected
	- Connection failure detection is rely on websocket close signal
	  in the commit. The VccConnectionHandler with its architecture
	  is fairly easy to include additional network failure detection
	  method E.g. heartbeat

   < f73917c, Brian Peters, 2020-09-14 14:13:04 -0400 >
   - Rename State enum to CallState, and WebCall 'statev' to 'state' 
   The State enum was ported from a nested enum inside CSSCall, but not that it is a top level enum in the Web client, it needs a prefix to specify what the state is for, so we will now call it 'CallState'.

The 'v' part of 'statev' was part of a naming scheme introduced in the original Modula implementation, and is not applicatble in the Web implementation. So, we drop the 'v' suffix from the name.

   < 4250c32, Brian Peters, 2022-12-13 14:03:35 -0500 >
   - PWEB-2710: add support for outbound SIP uri dialing in WebLine.makeCall() 
   - in WebLine.makeCall(), detect when dial address is a SIP uri, and avoid test for "Hookflash"

   < 5fa536e, Stephane Legris, 2022-06-03 09:43:08 -0400 >
   - PWEB-2391/PWEB-2401: Add new SIP Register and, an outgoing SIP BYE header. 
   PWEB-2391: The new SIP REGISTER header called "x-CallReofferRequired" will be process by the node to REOFFER all calls related to that position after a WebRTCGw switch over connection.

PWEB-2401: Add a new SIP header called "x-IgnoreBye" when terminating the session.  This new header will be processed by "sip.js" when terminating sessions of the failed WebRTCGw client in order to terminate cleanly all the sessions without sending the SIP BYE.
Please note the SIP BYE, if reaching the node, will terminate the 911 call which we want to keep alive.  This situation may occurs if the WebRTCGw network connection is CUT for a short period of time..

1.5.0.6 - Released 2022/03/23 15:31:04

   < 4e38119, Brian Peters, 2022-03-23 14:20:04 -0400 >
   - PWEB-2085: remove state transition to IHold when connecting consultation call to held conference 
   - when connecting a consultation call from a Normal (sameline) conference, the order of operations is for the consultation call to join the conference, and to UnHold the conference.
- This means the consultation call was going from Connected state in the private consultation conference, to IHold when joining the main conference, to Connected again once the main conference is re-connected (unhold).
- The additional temporary state transition to IHold was causing issued at the P911 GUI level, because no call in the conference was considered "Connected" for a brief moment, and triggered a cleanup of state.
- To avoid this, the consulation call will remain in the Connected state in the on-hold conference, even if this is internally inconsistent, since we know it will become consistent again once all the other calls are Connected by the confernence UnHold at the end of the conference Connect() operation

   < 3889878, Stephane Legris, 2022-03-21 10:22:06 -0400 >
   - PWEB-1607: Add a comment only about the sip.js constant name.

1.4.0.10 - Released 2022/03/02 15:02:05

   < 615c450, Brian Peters, 2022-02-23 08:28:52 -0500 >
   - PWEB-1844: improve LineLock race condition handling in WebCall.answer() 
   - add 500ms delay to callTerminated() promise handling in WebCall.answer() to allow for CallLink event to arrive, which will tell us if LineLock happened
- re-validate the call state after the async operation to hold current connected calls, and Listen & Join cancel, since the state may have changed
- add another level of try/catch for better cleanup of ForceConnectSync
- while testing, we noticed that the SIP.js library didn't always properly handle the race condition of sending the 200 OK from accept() while being Cancelled from the server. In some cases, the call to invitation.accept() promise *never resolves*, which caused our WebPhone.answer() wrapper to also never resolve and leave the app in a state where it could no longer accept calls. A timeout for the WebPhone.answer() was added in WebCall.answer() so the operation always resolves and proper cleanup is done
- in WebLineDev.processCallIncoming(), which is not async, catch the exceptions from the async calls to webCall.reject() and WebCall.answer() and log them

1.2.0.25 - Released 2021/08/05 10:51:46

   < 7117d37, Michael Ma, 2021-08-04 14:24:50 -0400 >
   - PWEB-1643, this commit is to avoid throwing exception "NotExist" on AcdLogOff 
   	- A rare and unusual situaion is seen in single node that Voip
	  probably cleaned up its ACD database prior to acdLogout
	  request. This might be because the webClient is pausing and
	  blocking Sip options to send so that Asterisk thinks it's not
	  reachable then cleaned-up database instead. If the web client
	  operates ACD logOff, the Vcc response 'NotExist' will be
	  received and it triggers an exception. This result could
	  potentially prevent PWEB GUI from exit on clicking shutdown
	  button. Response 'NotExist' can be considered as a success of ACD
	  logoff. Since Asterisk does have a seperate way to clean-up
	  its database, we need to take this unusual case as a possibility
	  to cover, which do not throw exception when it's resulted by
	  logout operation
	- Same logic applied to rgLougout in telephony code
	- Also add 'Unknown' ACD and RG opStatus to replace the case of
	  throwing exception if none of pre-defined status in
	  telephony matches what is recieved in the response of ACD or
	  RG OP

   < 7a5eb18, Stephane Legris, 2021-07-29 15:44:57 -0400 >
   - [L&J] PWEB-1579 Resubscribe expires is now 1h 
   
   < b818c4b, Stephane Legris, 2021-07-29 15:17:13 -0400 >
   - [L&J] PWEB-1579: Resubscribe alternative solution 
   - The NTimer or expires is now set to 1h..  Therefore, the L&J will last 1h+ before terminating
- When subscribe unexpected terminated state is received, we terminate the current call if applicable, unsubscribe all nodes BUT, we DO NOT reset current L&J and, DO NOT report event status to the GUI
- Then, we silently start a new monitoring with the same L&J settings.  If a L&J monitoring call was active, the node will then send another NOTIFY to re-establish the call to listen or join the position or AgentID to monitor.
- The whole recovery cycle transition takes about 4-5 seconds.  So, the supervisor will stop earring the position or AgentID for that duration.
- When that L&J re-cycle occurs. The following ERROR message is displayed on the console:  "subscribe <index> UNEXPECTEDLY terminated.  Restart it silently !
- Also, if by any chance, a L&J subscribe is kept alive within a Node, the next subscribe will destroy it.  Furthermore, if a notify is sent by this node, PWEB returns a “481 dialog does not exist”.

1.1.0.4 - Released 2021/03/05 16:10:51

   < c8af719, Michael Ma, 2021-03-05 15:49:23 -0500 >
   - PWEB-1196 This commit adds support for multiple VCC GW 
   	- Add VccConnectionHandler to Telephony
	- VccConnectionHandler initally establishes a handles list. Each
	  handle represents the connection and vccClient to a VccGW
	  respectively. It connects/re-connects and creates vccClient and
	  update to lineDev to be effective immediately once it's chosen
	- When a connection close discovered, try with the rest handles in
	  the list at the order of what is configured. The handle to the
	  conection that was just closed is excluded from rest handles list
	  unless it's the only one configured in the system
	- All failure will rerult in a retry over the handles list every
	  10 seconds until one got connected
	- Connection failure detection is rely on websocket close signal
	  in the commit. The VccConnectionHandler with its architecture
	  is fairly easy to include additional network failure detection
	  method E.g. heartbeat

   < dcdfc44, Daouda Taha, 2021-03-04 17:27:37 -0500 >
